mm=maint['completed'].str.split(':').str[1].astype(int)\nmaint['completed_min']=maint['day']*1440 + hh*60 + mm\nmaint=maint.sort_values(['machine_id','completed_min'])\nmaint['window_idx']=maint.groupby('machine_id').cumcount()\n\nb=pd.read_csv(root/'production_batches.csv')\nma=pd.read_csv(root/'machine_assignment_log.csv')\nq=pd.read_csv(root/'quality_inspections.csv')\nprod=pd.read_csv(root/'products.csv')\nb=b.merge(ma[['day','job_id','machine_id','start_time']], left_on=['production_day','job_id','machine_id'], right_on=['day','job_id','machine_id'], how='left')\nhh=b['start_time'].str.split(':').str[0].astype(int); mm=b['start_time'].str.split(':').str[1].astype(int)\nb['start_min']=b['production_day']*1440 + hh*60 + mm\nparts=[]\nfor machine, g in b.sort_values(['machine_id','start_min']).groupby('machine_id', sort=False):\n    m=maint[maint.machine_id==machine].sort_values('completed_min')\n    parts.append(pd.merge_asof(g.sort_values('start_min'), m[['completed_min','work_order_id','technician_id','window_idx']], left_on='start_min', right_on='completed_min', direction='backward'))\nassigned=pd.concat(parts, ignore_index=True).merge(q[['batch_id','inspection_result','rejected_pct']], on='batch_id').merge(prod[['product_id','quality_rejection_threshold_pct']], on='product_id')\nassigned=assigned[assigned.work_order_id.notna()].copy()\nassigned['margin']=assigned['rejected_pct']-assigned['quality_rejection_threshold_pct']\nassigned['is_reject']=assigned['inspection_result'].eq('REJECTED')\nprod_stats=assigned.groupby('product_id')['margin'].agg(['mean','std']).rename(columns={'mean':'prod_mean','std':'prod_std'})\nwp=assigned.groupby(['machine_id','window_idx','work_order_id','technician_id','product_id']).agg(batches=('batch_id','count'), rejects=('is_reject','sum'), mean_margin=('margin','mean'), max_margin=('margin','max'), min_margin=('margin','min')).reset_index().merge(prod_stats, on='product_id')\nwp['z_mean']=(wp['mean_margin']-wp['prod_mean'])/wp['prod_std']\nfor z in [3,4,5]:\n    good=wp[(wp.rejects>0)&(wp.z_mean>=z)]\n    tech=good.groupby('technician_id').agg(rej=('rejects','sum'), wos=('work_order_id','nunique')).sort_values(['rej','wos'], ascending=False)\n    confirmed=tech[(tech.rej>=3)&(tech.wos>=2)]\n    mapping=good[good.technician_id.isin(confirmed.index)].groupby('product_id')['technician_id'].apply(lambda s: sorted(set(s))).to_dict()\n    print('=== z',z)\n    print('confirmed techs', confirmed.to_string())\n    print('mapping', json.dumps(mapping, sort_keys=True))\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}

{"type":"item.started","item":{"id":"item_28","type":"command_execution","command":"/bin/bash -lc \"python - <<'PY'\nimport pandas as pd, pathlib, numpy as np\nroot=pathlib.Path('/app')\n# parse maintenance\nrows=[]\nfor path in root.joinpath('raw_service_reports').rglob('*_service.txt'):\n    rec={}\n    for line in path.read_text().splitlines():\n        if ': ' in line:\n            k,v=line.split(': ',1)\n            rec[k]=v\n    rows.append({'day': int(rec['DAY']), 'work_order_id': rec['WORK ORDER'], 'machine_id': rec['MACHINE'], 'technician_id': rec['TECHNICIAN'], 'completed': rec['COMPLETED']})\nmaint=pd.DataFrame(rows)\nhh=maint['completed'].str.split(':').str[0].astype(int); mm=maint['completed'].str.split(':').str[1].astype(int)\nmaint['completed_min']=maint['day']*1440 + hh*60 + mm\nmaint=maint.sort_values(['machine_id','completed_min'])\nmaint['window_idx']=maint.groupby('machine_id').cumcount()\n\nb=pd.read_csv(root/'production_batches.csv')\nma=pd.read_csv(root/'machine_assignment_log.csv')\nq=pd.read_csv(root/'quality_inspections.csv')\nprod=pd.read_csv(root/'products.csv')\nb=b.merge(ma[['day','job_id','machine_id','start_time']], left_on=['production_day','job_id','machine_id'], right_on=['day','job_id','machine_id'], how='left')\nhh=b['start_time'].str.split(':').str[0].astype(int); mm=b['start_time'].str.split(':').str[1].astype(int)\nb['start_min']=b['production_day']*1440 + hh*60 + mm\nparts=[]\nfor machine, g in b.sort_values(['machine_id','start_min']).groupby('machine_id', sort=False):\n    m=maint[maint.machine_id==machine].sort_values('completed_min')\n    parts.append(pd.merge_asof(g.sort_values('start_min'), m[['completed_min','work_order_id','technician_id','window_idx']], left_on='start_min', right_on='completed_min', direction='backward'))\nassigned=pd.concat(parts, ignore_index=True).merge(q[['batch_id','inspection_result','rejected_pct']], on='batch_id').merge(prod[['product_id','quality_rejection_threshold_pct']], on='product_id')\nassigned=assigned[assigned.work_order_id.notna()].copy()\nassigned['margin']=assigned['rejected_pct']-assigned['quality_rejection_threshold_pct']\nassigned['is_reject']=assigned['inspection_result'].eq('REJECTED').astype(int)\nprod_stats=assigned.groupby('product_id')['margin'].agg(['mean','std']).rename(columns={'mean':'prod_mean','std':'prod_std'})\nwp=assigned.groupby(['machine_id','window_idx','work_order_id','technician_id','product_id']).agg(batches=('batch_id','count'), rejects=('is_reject','sum'), mean_margin=('margin','mean'), max_margin=('margin','max')).reset_index().merge(prod_stats, on='product_id')\nwp['z_mean']=(wp['mean_margin']-wp['prod_mean'])/wp['prod_std']\n# neighbor stats\nrecords=[]\nfor (machine, prod_id), g in wp.sort_values('window_idx').groupby(['machine_id','product_id']):\n    g=g.sort_values('window_idx').reset_index(drop=True)\n    prev_mean=[]; next_mean=[]; prev_rej=[]; next_rej=[]; prev_idx=[]; next_idx=[]\n    for i in range(len(g)):\n        prev = g.iloc[max(0,i-2):i]\n        nxt = g.iloc[i+1:i+3]\n        prev_mean.append(prev['mean_margin'].mean() if len(prev) else np.nan)\n        next_mean.append(nxt['mean_margin'].mean() if len(nxt) else np.nan)\n        prev_rej.append(prev['rejects'].sum() if len(prev) else np.nan)\n        next_rej.append(nxt['rejects'].sum() if len(nxt) else np.nan)\n        prev_idx.append(prev['window_idx'].max() if len(prev) else np.nan)\n        next_idx.append(nxt['window_idx'].min() if len(nxt) else np.nan)\n    g=g.assign(prev_mean=prev_mean,next_mean=next_mean,prev_rej=prev_rej,next_rej=next_rej,prev_idx=prev_idx,next_idx=next_idx)\n    records.append(g)\nwp2=pd.concat(records, ignore_index=True)\nwp2['spike_prev']=(wp2['mean_margin']-wp2['prev_mean'])/wp2['prod_std']\nwp2['spike_next']=(wp2['mean_margin']-wp2['next_mean'])/wp2['prod_std']\n# list rejected windows with spikes\nx=wp2[wp2.rejects>0].copy()\nprint(x.sort_values(['z_mean','spike_prev','spike_next'], ascending=False).head(120).to_string(index=False))\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}

mm=maint['completed'].str.split(':').str[1].astype(int)\nmaint['completed_min']=maint['day']*1440 + hh*60 + mm\nmaint=maint.sort_values(['machine_id','completed_min'])\nmaint['window_idx']=maint.groupby('machine_id').cumcount()\n\nb=pd.read_csv(root/'production_batches.csv')\nma=pd.read_csv(root/'machine_assignment_log.csv')\nq=pd.read_csv(root/'quality_inspections.csv')\nprod=pd.read_csv(root/'products.csv')\nb=b.merge(ma[['day','job_id','machine_id','start_time']], m[['completed_min','work_order_id','technician_id','window_idx']], left_on='start_min', right_on='completed_min', direction='backward'))\nassigned=pd.concat(parts, on='product_id')\nassigned=assigned[assigned.work_order_id.notna()].copy()\nassigned['margin']=assigned['rejected_pct']-assigned['quality_rejection_threshold_pct']\nassigned['is_reject']=assigned['inspection_result'].eq('REJECTED').astype(int)\nprod_stats=assigned.groupby('product_id')['margin'].agg(['mean','std']).rename(columns={'mean':'prod_mean','std':'prod_std'})\nwp=assigned.groupby(['machine_id','window_idx','work_order_id','technician_id','product_id']).agg(batches=('batch_id','count'), rejects=('is_reject','sum'), mean_margin=('margin','mean'), max_margin=('margin','max')).reset_index().merge(prod_stats, causal.add(int(g.loc[i,'index']))\n    good=wp.loc[list(causal)].copy()\n    tech=good.groupby('technician_id').agg(rej=('rejects','sum'), wos=('work_order_id','nunique')).sort_values(['rej','wos'], {"type":"item.started","item":{"id":"item_31","type":"command_execution","command":"/bin/bash -lc \"python - <<'PY'\nimport pandas as pd, pathlib\nroot=pathlib.Path('/app')\n# setup parsing\nrows=[]\nfor path in root.joinpath('raw_service_reports').rglob('*_service.txt'):\n    rec={}\n    for line in path.read_text().splitlines():\n        if ': ' in line:\n            k,v=line.split(': ',1)\n            rec[k]=v\n    rows.append({'day': int(rec['DAY']), 'work_order_id': rec['WORK ORDER'], 'machine_id': rec['MACHINE'], 'technician_id': rec['TECHNICIAN'], 'completed': rec['COMPLETED']})\nmaint=pd.DataFrame(rows)\nhh=maint['completed'].str.split(':').str[0].astype(int); mm=maint['completed'].str.split(':').str[1].astype(int)\nmaint['completed_min']=maint['day']*1440 + hh*60 + mm\nmaint=maint.sort_values(['machine_id','completed_min'])\nmaint['window_idx']=maint.groupby('machine_id').cumcount()\n\nb=pd.read_csv(root/'production_batches.csv')\nma=pd.read_csv(root/'machine_assignment_log.csv')\nq=pd.read_csv(root/'quality_inspections.csv')\nprod=pd.read_csv(root/'products.csv')\nb=b.merge(ma[['day','job_id','machine_id','start_time']], left_on=['production_day','job_id','machine_id'], right_on=['day','job_id','machine_id'], how='left')\nhh=b['start_time'].str.split(':').str[0].astype(int); mm=b['start_time'].str.split(':').str[1].astype(int)\nb['start_min']=b['production_day']*1440 + hh*60 + mm\nparts=[]\nfor machine, g in b.sort_values(['machine_id','start_min']).groupby('machine_id', sort=False):\n    m=maint[maint.machine_id==machine].sort_values('completed_min')\n    parts.append(pd.merge_asof(g.sort_values('start_min'), m[['completed_min','work_order_id','technician_id','window_idx']], left_on='start_min', right_on='completed_min', direction='backward'))\nassigned=pd.concat(parts, ignore_index=True).merge(q[['batch_id','inspection_result','rejected_pct']], on='batch_id').merge(prod[['product_id','quality_rejection_threshold_pct']], on='product_id')\nassigned=assigned[assigned.work_order_id.notna()].copy()\nassigned['margin']=assigned['rejected_pct']-assigned['quality_rejection_threshold_pct']\nassigned['is_reject']=assigned['inspection_result'].eq('REJECTED').astype(int)\nprod_stats=assigned.groupby('product_id')['margin'].agg(['mean','std']).rename(columns={'mean':'prod_mean','std':'prod_std'})\nwp=assigned.groupby(['machine_id','window_idx','work_order_id','technician_id','product_id']).agg(batches=('batch_id','count'), rejects=('is_reject','sum'), mean_margin=('margin','mean'), max_margin=('margin','max')).reset_index().merge(prod_stats, on='product_id')\nwp['z_mean']=(wp['mean_margin']-wp['prod_mean'])/wp['prod_std']\n# compute local spike as before\nrecords=[]\nfor (machine, prod_id), g in wp.sort_values('window_idx').groupby(['machine_id','product_id']):\n    g=g.sort_values('window_idx').reset_index(drop=True)\n    prev_mean=[]; next_mean=[]\n    for i in range(len(g)):\n        prev=g.iloc[max(0,i-2):i]; nxt=g.iloc[i+1:i+3]\n        prev_mean.append(prev['mean_margin'].mean() if len(prev) else None)\n        next_mean.append(nxt['mean_margin'].mean() if len(nxt) else None)\n    g=g.assign(prev_mean=prev_mean,next_mean=next_mean)\n    records.append(g)\nwp=pd.concat(records, ignore_index=True)\nwp['spike_prev']=(wp['mean_margin']-wp['prev_mean'])/wp['prod_std']\nwp['spike_next']=(wp['mean_margin']-wp['next_mean'])/wp['prod_std']\ntechs=['TECH_002','TECH_003','TECH_004','TECH_014','TECH_021','TECH_027','TECH_030','TECH_031','TECH_032','TECH_037','TECH_041']\nfor tech in techs:\n    print('===',tech)\n    print(wp[(wp.technician_id==tech)&(wp.rejects>0)].sort_values(['product_id','window_idx'])[['machine_id','window_idx','work_order_id','product_id','batches','rejects','mean_margin','z_mean','spike_prev','spike_next']].to_string(index=False))\n    print()\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}

{"type":"item.started","item":{"id":"item_34","type":"command_execution","command":"/bin/bash -lc \"python - <<'PY'\nimport pandas as pd, pathlib, math\nroot=pathlib.Path('/app')\n# parse maintenance\nrows=[]\nfor path in root.joinpath('raw_service_reports').rglob('*_service.txt'):\n    rec={}\n    for line in path.read_text().splitlines():\n        if ': ' in line:\n            k,v=line.split(': ',1)\n            rec[k]=v\n    rows.append({'day': int(rec['DAY']), 'work_order_id': rec['WORK ORDER'], 'machine_id': rec['MACHINE'], 'technician_id': rec['TECHNICIAN'], 'completed': rec['COMPLETED']})\nmaint=pd.DataFrame(rows)\nhh=maint['completed'].str.split(':').str[0].astype(int); mm=maint['completed'].str.split(':').str[1].astype(int)\nmaint['completed_min']=maint['day']*1440 + hh*60 + mm\nmaint=maint.sort_values(['machine_id','completed_min'])\n\nb=pd.read_csv(root/'production_batches.csv')\nma=pd.read_csv(root/'machine_assignment_log.csv')\nq=pd.read_csv(root/'quality_inspections.csv')\nb=b.merge(ma[['day','job_id','machine_id','start_time']], left_on=['production_day','job_id','machine_id'], right_on=['day','job_id','machine_id'], how='left')\nhh=b['start_time'].str.split(':').str[0].astype(int); mm\nmaint=maint.sort_values(['machine_id','completed_min'])\nmaint['window_idx']=maint.groupby('machine_id').cumcount()\n\nb=pd.read_csv(root/'production_batches.csv')\nma=pd.read_csv(root/'machine_assignment_log.csv')\nq=pd.read_csv(root/'quality_inspections.csv')\nprod=pd.read_csv(root/'products.csv')\nb=b.merge(ma[['day','job_id','machine_id','start_time']], left_on=['production_day','job_id','machine_id'], right_on=['day','job_id','machine_id'], how='left')\nhh=b['start_time'].str.split(':').str[0].astype(int); mm=b['start_time'].str.split(':').str[1].astype(int)\nb['start_min']=b['production_day']*1440 + hh*60 + mm\nparts=[]\nfor machine, g in b.sort_values(['machine_id','start_min']).groupby('machine_id', m[['completed_min','work_order_id','technician_id','window_idx']], left_on='start_min', right_on='completed_min', direction='backward'))\nassigned=pd.concat(parts, ignore_index=True).merge(q[['batch_id','inspection_result','rejected_pct']], on='batch_id').merge(prod[['product_id','quality_rejection_threshold_pct']], on='product_id')\nassigned=assigned[assigned.work_order_id.notna()].copy()\nassigned['margin']=assigned['rejected_pct']-assigned['quality_rejection_threshold_pct']\nassigned['is_reject']=assigned['inspection_result'].eq('REJECTED').astype(int)\nprod_stats=assigned.groupby('product_id')['margin'].agg(['mean','std']).rename(columns={'mean':'prod_mean','std':'prod_std'})\nwp=assigned.groupby(['machine_id','window_idx','work_order_id','technician_id','product_id']).agg(batches=('batch_id','count'), rejects=('is_reject','sum'), mean_margin=('margin','mean'), max_margin=('margin','max')).reset_index().merge(prod_stats, on='product_id')\nwp['z_mean']=(wp['mean_margin']-wp['prod_mean'])/wp['prod_std']\n# work order z\nprod_rate=assigned.groupby('product_id')['is_reject'].mean().to_dict()\nassigned['exp_p']=assigned['product_id'].map(prod_rate)\nwo=assigned.groupby(['work_order_id']).agg(expected=('exp_p','sum'), rejects=('is_reject','sum')).reset_index()\nvar=assigned.assign(var=lambda d: d.exp_p*(1-d.exp_p)).groupby('work_order_id')['var'].sum().reset_index()\nwo=wo.merge(var,on='work_order_id')\nwo['wo_z']=(wo['rejects']-wo['expected'])/wo['var']**0.5\nwp=wp.merge(wo[['work_order_id','wo_z']], on='work_order_id')\n# classify\nwp['causal']=False\n# strong per product-window\nwp.loc[(wp.rejects>0) & ((wp.z_mean>=2.5) | ((wp.rejects>=2) & (wp.mean_margin>-0.01))), 'causal']=True\n# work-order anomalous rescue for positive-mean rejected products\nwp.loc[(wp.rejects>0) & (wp.wo_z>=4.5) & (wp.mean_margin>0), 'causal']=True\n# chain extension across consecutive observed reject windows same machine/product if one in chain causal and current mean_margin>-0.005\nfor (machine, prod_id), g in wp.sort_values('window_idx').groupby(['machine_id','product_id']):\n    g=g.sort_values('window_idx')\n    idxs=g.index.tolist()\n    # observed reject windows chain contiguous in observed sequence\n    reject_positions=[i for i,row in g.iterrows() if row.rejects>0]\n    if not reject_positions:\n        continue\n    pos_to_seq={idx:pos for pos,idx in enumerate(g.index)}\n    # build contiguous groups in observed order among reject windows\n    current=[]; prev_pos=None\n    for idx in reject_positions:\n        pos=pos_to_seq[idx]\n        if prev_pos is None or pos==prev_pos+1:\n            current.append(idx)\n        else:\n            if any(wp.loc[current,'causal']):\n                for j in current:\n                    if wp.loc[j,'mean_margin']>-0.005:\n                        wp.loc[j,'causal']=True\n            current=[idx]\n        prev_pos=pos\n    if current and any(wp.loc[current,'causal']):\n        for j in current:\n            if wp.loc[j,'mean_margin']>-0.005:\n                wp.loc[j,'causal']=True\n\ngood=wp[wp.causal].copy()\ntech=good.groupby('technician_id').agg(rej=('rejects','sum'), wos=('work_order_id','nunique')).sort_values(['rej','wos'], ascending=False)\nconfirmed=tech[(tech.rej>=3)&(tech.wos>=2)]\nprint('confirmed\\\\n',confirmed)\nprint('\\\\ncausal windows for confirmed')\nprint(good[good.technician_id.isin(confirmed.index)].sort_values(['technician_id','product_id','work_order_id'])[['technician_id','work_order_id','machine_id','product_id','batches','rejects','mean_margin','z_mean','wo_z']].to_string(index=False))\nmapping=good[good.technician_id.isin(confirmed.index)].groupby('product_id')['technician_id'].apply(lambda s: sorted(set(s))).to_dict()\nprint('\\\\nmapping',json.dumps(mapping, sort_keys=True))\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}

on='product_id')\nwp['z_mean']=(wp['mean_margin']-wp['prod_mean'])/wp['prod_std']\n# work order
